###  Voivuori₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Voivuori* (butter mountain)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  24
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
